   sa kṛtvā rājasaṃ tyāgaṃ naiva tyāgaphalaṃ labhet ||8||	sa kRtvA rAjasam tyAgam na-eva tyAga-Palam laBet ||8||
   Śrīdhara : rājasaṃ tyāgam āha duḥkham iti | yaḥ kartā ātma-bodhaṃ vinā	ŚrIDara : rAjasam tyAgam Aha duHKam iti | yaH kartA Atma--boDam vinA
   kevalaṃ duḥkham ity evaṃ matvā śarīrāyāsa-bhayāt nityaṃ karma tyajet iti	kevalam duHKam iti evam matvA SarIra-AyAsa--BayAt nityam karma tyajet iti
   yat tādṛśas tyāgo rājaso duḥkhasya rājasatvāt | atas taṃ rājasaṃ tyāgaṃ	yat tAdRSaH tyAgaH rAjasaH duHKasya rAja-satvAt | atas tam rAjasam tyAgam
   kṛtvā sa rājasaḥ puruṣas tyāgasya phalaṃ jñāna-niṣṭhā-lakṣaṇaṃ naiva	kRtvA sa rAjasaH puruzaH tyAgasya Palam jQAna--nizWA--lakzaNam na-eva
   labhata ity arthaḥ ||8||	laBate iti arTaH ||8||
   Viśvanātha : duḥkham ity eveti | yadyapi nitya-karmaṇām āvaśyakam eva	ViSvanATa : duHKam iti eva-iti | yadi-api nitya-karmaNAm AvaSyakam eva
   tat-karaṇe guṇa eva na tu doṣa iti jānāmy eva | tad apii taiḥ śarīraṃ mayā	tat-karaNe guNaH eva na tu dozaH iti jAnAmi eva | tat apii tEH SarIram mayA

   dravopyārjana-prātaḥ-snānādinā duḥkha-rūpam iti kāya-kleśa-bhayāc caitan	drava-upya-arjana--prAtaH--snAna-AdinA duHKa-rUpam iti kAya--kleSa--BayAt ca-etat-
   mumukṣur api tyajet | sa tyāgo rājasaḥ duḥkhasya rajo-dharmatvāt | taṃ	mumukzuH api tyajet | sa tyAgaH rAjasaH duHKasya rajo-Darma-tvAt | tam
   tyāgaṃ kṛtvāpi janas tasya phalaṃ jñāna-niṣṭhāṃ na labheta ||8||	tyAgam kRtvA-api janaH tasya Palam jQAna---nizWAm na laBeta ||8||
   BhG 18.9	Bhu 18.9

   Śrīdhara : sāttvikaṃ tyāgam āha kāryam iti | kāryam ity evaṃ niyatam	ŚrIDara : sAttvikam tyAgam Aha kAryam iti | kAryam iti evam niyatam

   BhG 18.10	Bhu 18.10

   BhG 18.11	Bhu 18.11

   tyāgīty abhidhīyate ||11||	tyAgI-iti aBiDIyate ||11||
   Viśvanātha : ito 'pi śāstrīyaṃ karma na tyājyam ity āha na hīti | tyaktuṃ	ViSvanATa : itas api SAstrI-iyam karma na tyAjyam iti Aha na hi-iti | tyaktum

   BhG 18.12	Bhu 18.12
   aniṣṭam iṣṭaṃ miśraṃ ca trividhaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam |	anizwam izwam miSram ca triviDam karmaNaH Palam |

   Śrīdhara : evambhūtasya karma-phala-tyāgasya phalam āha aniṣṭam iti |	ŚrIDara : evamBUtasya karma-Pala--tyAgasya Palam Aha anizwam iti |

   karma-phalam | atyāginām ukta-tyāga-rahitānāṃ pretya para-kāle bhavati |	karma--Palam | atyAginAm ukta-tyAga--rahitAnAm pretya para-kAle Bavati |

   BhG 18.13	Bhu 18.13
   pañcaitāni mahābāho kāraṇāni nibodha me |	paQca-etAni mahA-bAho kAraNAni niboDa me |

   sāṅkhya iti | sāṅkhyaṃ jñānaṃ tat-pratipādakaṃ vedānta-śāstram sāṅkhyaṃ	sAFKyaH iti | sAFKyam jQAnam tat--pratipAdakam vedAnta-SAstram sAFKyam

   BhG 18.14	Bhu 18.14

   yad icchā-tariṃ prāpya gītāpayodhau	yat icCA-A-tarim prApya gIta-apayoDO
   nyamajjaṃ gṛhītāti-citrārtha-ratnam |	nyamajjam gRhIta-ati-citra-arTa-ratnam |

   sa me kautukī nanda-sūnuḥ priyastāt ||	sa me kOtukI nanda-sUnuH priyaH-tAt ||
   śrīmad-gītā-bhūṣaṇaṃ nāma bhāṣyaṃ	SrImad-gItA-BUzaNam nAma BAzyam
   yatnād vidyā-bhūṣaṇenopacīrṇam |	yatnAt vidyA--BUzaNena-upacIrNam |
   śrī-govinda-prema-mādhurya-lubdhāḥ	SrI---govinda--prema--mADurya--lubDAH
   kāruṇyārdrāḥ sādhavaḥ śodhayadhvam ||	kAruNya-ArdrAH sADavaH SoDayaDvam ||
   iti śrīmad-bhagavad-gītopaniṣad-bhāṣye 'ṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||	iti SrI-mat--Bagavat--gIta-upanizad--BAzye azwAdaSaH aDyAyaH ||
